	|	<block terminal definitions> <block terminal definition> 
	;


<block terminal definition>
	:	<attribute list optional> <terminal definition> 
	;


<block regex definitions>
	:	<block regex definition> 
	|	<block regex definitions> <block regex definition> 
	;


<block regex definition>
	:	<attribute list optional> <regex definition> 
	;


<scanner part>
	:	<attribute list optional> '%scanner' <identifier> '%{' <regular expression list optional> '%}' 
	;


<regular expression list>
	:	<regular expression usage> 
	|	<regular expression list> <regular expression usage> 
	;


<regular expression usage>
	:	<regular expression> <actions optional> 
	;


<actions>
	:	<action> 
	|	<actions> <action> 
	;


<action>
	:	<skip action> 
	|	<terminal action> 
	|	<event action> 
	|	<push action> 
	|	<pop action> 
	;


<skip action>
	:	'skip' 
	;


<terminal action>
	:	'terminal' <identifier> 
	;


<event action>
	:	'event' <identifier> 
	;


<push action>
	:	'push' <identifier> 
	;


<pop action>
	:	'pop' 
	;


<lexer part>
	:	<attribute list optional> '%lexer' <identifier> '%{' <attribute list optional> '%}' 
	;


<parser part>
	:	<attribute list optional> '%parser' <identifier> '%{' <anglr syntax rule list optional> '%}' 
	;


<anglr syntax rule list>
	:	<anglr syntax rule> 
	|	<anglr syntax rule list> <anglr syntax rule> 
	;


<anglr syntax rule>
	:	<attribute list optional> <identifier> ':' <anglr syntax production list> ';' 
	|	<attribute list optional> <identifier> '{' <anglr syntax rule list optional> '}' 
	;


<anglr nested rule>
	:	<anglr syntax production list name optional> <anglr syntax production list> 
	;


<anglr syntax production list name>
	:	':' <identifier> ':' 
	;


<anglr syntax production list>
	:	<anglr syntax production> 
	|	<anglr syntax production list> '|' <anglr syntax production>  Left
	;


<anglr syntax production>
	:	<production name optional> <name list> <priority assoc specification optional> 
	|	'%empty' 
	;


<production name>
	:	'@@' <identifier> 
	;


<priority assoc specification>
	:	<priority specification> <associativity specification> 
	|	<associativity specification> <priority specification> 
	|	<priority specification> 
	|	<associativity specification> 
	|	<priority specification> ',' <associativity specification> 
	|	<associativity specification> ',' <priority specification> 
	;


<priority specification>
	:	'%priority' <number> 
	|	'%priority' '=' <number> 
	;


<associativity specification>
	:	'%associativity' <cstring> 
	|	'%associativity' '=' <cstring> 
	|	'%associativity' <identifier> 
	|	'%associativity' '=' <identifier> 
	;


<name list>
	:	<marker list optional> 
	|	<name list> <g name> <marker list optional>  Left
	;


<marker list>
	:	<marker> 
	|	<marker list> <marker> 
	;


<marker>
	:	'@' <identifier> 
	;


<g name>
	:	<name> 
	|	'(' <anglr nested rule> ')' 
	|	<g name> <cardinality delimiter> 
	;


<name>
	:	<any> 
	|	<cstring> 
	|	<identifier> 
	;


<cardinality delimiter>
	:	<cardinality> <delimiter optional> 
	;


<cardinality>
	:	'?' 
	|	'+' 
	|	'-' 
	|	'*' 
	|	'/' 
	|	'~+' 
	|	'~-' 
	|	'~*' 
	|	'~/' 
	|	'{' <number optional> ',' <number optional> '}' 
	;


<delimiter>
	:	'[' <anglr nested rule> ']' 
	;


<attribute list optional>
	:	%empty
	|	<attribute list> 
	;


<name value list optional>
	:	%empty
	|	<name value list> 
	;


<anglr file part list optional>
	:	%empty
	|	<anglr file part list> 
	;


<anglr definition list optional>
	:	%empty
	|	<anglr definition list> 
	;


<block terminal definitions optional>
	:	%empty
	|	<block terminal definitions> 
	;


<block regex definitions optional>
	:	%empty
	|	<block regex definitions> 
	;


<regular expression list optional>
	:	%empty
	|	<regular expression list> 
	;


<actions optional>
	:	%empty
	|	<actions> 
	;


<anglr syntax rule list optional>
	:	%empty
	|	<anglr syntax rule list> 
	;


<anglr syntax production list name optional>
	:	%empty
	|	<anglr syntax production list name> 
	;


<production name optional>
	:	%empty
	|	<production name> 
	;


<priority assoc specification optional>
	:	%empty
	|	<priority assoc specification> 
	;


<marker list optional>
	:	%empty
	|	<marker list> 
	;


<delimiter optional>
	:	%empty
	|	<delimiter> 
	;


<cstring optional>
	:	%empty
	|	<cstring> 
	;


<number optional>
	:	%empty
	|	<number> 
	;


$accept
	:	<anglr file fragment> $eof-token 
	;
